When a cargo is\nloaded for discharge in a U.S. Port, U.S. Customs require a unique Bill of\nLading number to be on the original(s) Bill(s) of Lading.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">First four characters \u2013\nofficial code given to ship owners<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Four or five characters\n\u2013 ship\u2019s call sign<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Next six characters \u2013\nBill of Lading Date, date/month/year i.e. 140209 (meaning 14th February 2009)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Final character \u2013\nnumeric character 1-9 assigned by person signing Bill of Lading on the day of\nissue and illustrating the consecutive number of original sets of Bills issued\non that date. If more than nine sets of original Bills of Lading are issued the\ncode should be continued by reverting to alphabetical characters commencing at\nA progressing to Z, therefore allowing 35 sets of bills to be issued on any one\nday.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Note This applies to\neach set of bills, so if three original bills are required for a parcel each\nwill have<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">the same number on the\noriginal, duplicate and triplicate original bills.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Examples\nof the above system are:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The \u201c COMPANY\u201d loads\none parcel for discharge in the USA. Any documents concerning this parcel (but\nin particular the cargo manifest completed on arrival in the USA) will have the\nfollowing code put on them:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">COMPELQG50402091 \u2013\nwhere:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">COMP is the four\ncharacter group given to COMPANY vessels<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">ELQG5 is the ship\u2019s call\nsign<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">040209 is the bill of\nlading date 4th February 2009<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">1 is the consecutive\nnumber of the bill or set of bills.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Those ships with 5\ncharacters in their call sign and loading greater than 9 parcels may be\nillustrated as follows:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">COMPANYMWSR6160109C\nwould be the 12th set of original bills issued by the Master of the \u201cMaltida\u201d\non the 16th January 1999.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The responsibility for\nproviding the \u201cunique number\u201d is the responsibility of the ship owner . Some\nthird party owners may have created their own system for their own ships.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>There may also be occasions where\nsub-Charterers require their own identifier. Masters are to ensure the\nidentifier is included within their cargo report<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Standard Carrier\nAlpha Code, is to identify freight carriers in computer systems and shipping\ndocuments such as Bill of Lading, Freight Bill, Packing List, and Purchase\nOrder. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">SCAC is also used to identify an ocean carrier or self-filing party,\nsuch as a freight forwarder, for the Automated Manifest System used by US\nCustoms and Border Protection for electronic import customs clearance and for\nmanifest transmission as per the USA's \"24 Hours Rule\" which requires\nthe carrier to transmit a cargo manifest to US Customs at least 24 hours prior\nto a vessel's departure at port of loading.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most major petroleum\ncompanies use the SCAC to identify the companies that pick up product at their\nterminals. Further, SCACs are required when doing business with all U.S.\nGovernment agencies and with many commercial shippers including, but not\nlimited to, those in the automobile, petroleum, forest products, and chemical\nindustries as well as suppliers to retail businesses and carriers engaged in\nrailroad piggyback trailer and ocean container drayage. SCACs are also required\nfor the Customs and Border Protection\u2019s Automated Commercial Environment (ACE),\nAutomated Manifest (AMS) and Pre-Arrival Processing (PAPS) Systems, and the\nSurface Transportation Board (formerly interstate Commerce Commission) tariff\nfiling system.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ezkaABJU2rY/UAbnporfIvI/AAAAAAAANtE/YYQ8bcHDccg/s1600/VADAKAYIL3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"283\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ezkaABJU2rY/UAbnporfIvI/AAAAAAAANtE/YYQ8bcHDccg/s320/VADAKAYIL3.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n29 YEARS IN COMMAND<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. It is the end of an era.<br />\n<br />\nHe was India's ONLY megastar--the phenomenon.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nAmitabh Bachchan can never surpass him.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nHe was lead man in 128 movies, with 15 consecutive super-hits, which is a record which is hard to beat.. He captivated with soft dialogue delivery.<br />\n<br />\nHe was the charmer, with a trademark disarming smile--the quintessential romantic. Girls would swoon in a heap &nbsp;on just seeing him. <br />\n<br />\nOld women would turn mushy -- such was his appeal as the ultimate \"desi lover\",&nbsp; soft-- caring- tender-- sensitive--<br />\n<br />\nGirls married his photos and put blood as sindhur.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nHis car used to be covered with lip-stick marks. <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nGirls&nbsp;proposed to him by writing passionate letters in blood. <br />\n<br />\nHe was the only Bollywood star who could generate frenzy and mass hysteria.&nbsp; Nothing was stage managed as is usual nowadays.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nKids adored their Haathi mere Saathi uncle. Even today the oldies get goose bumps when they hear the song \" roop tera mastana \"of Aradhana ( with Sharmila in wet clothes&nbsp;in front of the fire )<br />\n<br />\nFrom 1969 to 1971, it was a one horse race in Bollywood. Who could race against King Midas?<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nHe was NOT a star son.&nbsp; He had NO god mother like Indira Gandhi , who wrote a recommendation letter for Amitabh Bachchan.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">Can there be another, ever again?</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a The Basel Mission at Calicut took this technology and patented it in the name of German Jew&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Christian Frederick\nSchonbein who taught Chemistry at the University of Berlin.. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Much later in September\n1896, the super- genius Nikola Tesla who took keen interest in Vedic science , patented\nhis first ozone generator, and formed the Tesla Ozone Co. </span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tesla sold ozone machines and ozonated olive\noil to doctors for medical use.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\nYou will notice that till they enslaved India, the Christian white man&nbsp;was terribly short of original ideas.&nbsp; Suddenly average guys&nbsp;became genuises, in the 17th , 18th, 19th and 20th centuries..&nbsp; And we all were wondering, where is the catch?</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\nThey were in denial , till the IT age-- when the world famous Universities&nbsp;found that the Indians in the Electronics and Computer science strains really had superior grey matter.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-L0vWaLf-zR4/T_sPeEHyRxI/AAAAAAAANkk/PsEebRKnyI8/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-L0vWaLf-zR4/T_sPeEHyRxI/AAAAAAAANkk/PsEebRKnyI8/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 16pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong><span style=\"color: blue;\">CARGO TANK INTERNAL\nINSPECTION ON CHEMICAL TANKERS- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></strong></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-P15t5xw9YXA/T_sPxYA6QMI/AAAAAAAANks/FfYa0ButHMI/s1600/SAM_3678.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"300\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-P15t5xw9YXA/T_sPxYA6QMI/AAAAAAAANks/FfYa0ButHMI/s400/SAM_3678.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chemical tankers will\nclean the cargo tanks and associated pipeline systems prior to declaring NOR and\narrival at the load berth.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br /><br /><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In modern times , it is\nessential to take plenty of pictures from all angles , with all ports open to\nallow daylight in. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Once you load the\npictures it in your computer, you can be surprised that the camera has pinged\nwhat your eyes could not --- and you can zoom in too. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />A&nbsp;smart tank inspector knows the position of your tankcleaning machines, the blind sectors of the jet and if you gave given machine drops . &nbsp;He knows where to look.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Special attention\nshould be paid to the condition of the tank coating in the case of epoxy coated\ntanks and, in particular, to the presence of blisters and flaking of the\ncoating.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Unbroken blisters may\ncontain residues from an earlier cargo as will loose or flaking coating.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Depending on the\ncharterer or shipper requirements, the inspector may be asked to estimate the\npercentage of coating missing or damaged.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Reference to the\nvessel\u2019s previous cargoes can have a bearing on the further action required\nfrom the crew when determining the likely effect the condition of the coating\nmight have on the cargo to be loaded.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Attention should also\nbe paid to the cargo tank, pipes, drop lines, pump casings, suction wells and\nheating coils. These items can form shadow areas and often receive less than\nadequate attention during tank washing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Inspectors cannot, of\ncourse, visually inspect the internal condition of pipelines for their full\nlength and the inspection report should clearly state the applicable\nlimitations.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vent and inert gas\nlines are usually visible at the tank entry point and could contain prior\ncargos, polymerized material, or washing residues, that if present, could\ncontribute to contamination.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Deck lines will have\ndrain points and these should be opened in case residues from tank washing\noperations or prior cargos are present.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wall\nwash test by inspectors/ suryeyors :--<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank surfaces must be\ndry.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Discoloured or broken\ncoating sections on tank walls should be sampled as follows:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Where such areas are\nless than 20% of total surface area (excluding deckheads), the washings should\nbe included with those of the rest of the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Non typical areas\nshould be sampled and tested separately. Samples should be tested in a shore\nbased laboratory.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\nminimum number of areas to wall wash depends on the tank capacity.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank capacity less than\n500 cubic metres--<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span> 5 areas<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank capacity 500 to\n1000 cubic metres--<span style=\"mso-tab-count: 1;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span> 7 areas<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank capacity greater\nthat 1000 cubic metres--<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>9 areas<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Wall wash sampling\nprocedures may cause a previously gas free tank to develop an unsafe atmosphere\nand personal protective gear should always be worn and breathing apparatus may\nbe required.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are limitations\non the extent to which inspectors can visually inspect all parts of the loading\nsystem, vessel and shore, and so they will<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>inquire about the steps taken by the vessel to avoid or reduce the risk\nof contamination.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Loading/discharge\nmanifolds, vents, and inert gas lines<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>can only be inspected where visually accessible.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Extensive areas of the pump and piping\nsystems can only be assessed on the basis of information obtained from the\nChief Officer in respect of tank cleaning operations and previous cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Prior to loading \u201cfirst\nfoots\u201d in tanks , an initial shore line sample should be drawn and visually\nexamined to ensure the cargo is clean and bright and free of suspended matter.\nThis first foot sample at the manifold must be drawn with the manifold valve\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">SHUT</span> ( you cant do this for screw pumps and reciprocating piston pumps ) <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Subject to wall wash\ntests (where applicable) and receiving laboratory clearance, the vessel will\nthen be able to start loading \u201cfirst foots\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">First Foot samples are\nrequired to determine whether any contaminants within the vessels loading\nsystems have survived cleaning regimes that might have a detrimental effect on\nthe cargo to be loaded.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cargo\nTank Coating Suitability<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The following is\nto<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>understanding potential contamination\nproblems that may arise with chemical cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Zinc silicate, phenolic\nepoxies and pure epoxies are the most commonly used generic coating systems in\ncargo tanks for the carriage of chemicals.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They vary in their\nresistance to cargoes and all have limitations in carriage.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The principal\nlimitation in the use of zinc silicates is that they are only suitable in a\nnarrow pH<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">range of approximately\n5.0 to 9.0.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Phenolic epoxies are\ngenerally able to carry a wider range of low molecular weight cargoes and have\na higher free fatty acid resistance<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The cargo resistance of\ncoatings of the same generic type can vary between manufacturers and, hence,\nthe manufacturers Resistance Lists usually available aboard the vessel should\nbe consulted should there be any doubts as to suitability of any particular\ncargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Some coatings are\ntemperature sensitive.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Cargo carriage\nrequirements may require heating, and temperature control should match the\ncoating operability range.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Organic epoxy coatings\nhave the propensity to absorb cargoes during a loaded passage. The\ncontamination potential to a subsequent cargo is therefore considerable as:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Large quantities can be\nretained<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The amount retained\nafter different time periods is not well defined<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Variable\nabsorption/desorption characteristics are found between different coating types<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Variable\nabsorption/desorption characteristics are found within the same generic types\nfrom different manufacturers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Different rates of\nabsorption/desorption are found between different cargoes<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Factors such as coating\nthickness, temperature and tank cleaning also have an influence on absorption\nand desorption.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">With some chemical\ncargoes, absorbed material can survive both further intermediate cargoes as\nwell as extensive tank cleaning operations<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The shore tank\ninspector is NOT a bird. He goes down the tank ladder . On the way, he will\ntouch and rub certain areas. Be sure that these areas are good. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At the tank dome itself\n<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>, before entering , the shore surveyor <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>will smell the tank, and sometimes this smell\ncould come from dirty gasket of the tank dome cover. He will refuse to enter if\nthe previous cargo has any carcinogenic percentage .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cargo hoses used for\nlooping forms part of the pipelines . Number them and have a list of the last 3\ncargoes handles by these hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If the previous cargo\nwas insoluble in water, check the threads of all bolts inside the tank,\nminutely.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sometimes it so transpires\nthat after Methanol / potable Ethanol discharge, the tank was vented and the tank\nfails at the load port for the same cargo, to be loaded again. Just make sure\nthe horizontals and slanted surfaces do NOT have any sediment, by rubbing a wet\nblack/ white cotton lint free cloth.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nowadays surveyors are\nhand in glove with shippers ( for a ulterior&nbsp;reasons ) and they fail the tanks for moisture\ncondensation. Don\u2019t be na\u00efve. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><strong><span style=\"color: red;\">The\nprinciple to apply here is -- warm moist air, always condenses on a cold steel bulkhead</span></strong>.\nThis is the reason why chemical tanker-men cannot be dimwits.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dncSvdEuIsw/T_sPNaDU0dI/AAAAAAAANkc/5buiqw9zL7s/s1600/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-dncSvdEuIsw/T_sPNaDU0dI/AAAAAAAANkc/5buiqw9zL7s/s320/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">29 years in command <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; Revelation 1:6.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Melchizedek is mentioned twice in the Hebrew Bible, the first in Genesis and the second in Psalms.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Genesis 14:18 introduces Melchizedek a \"Priest of the Most High God\" (El Elyon), a term which is re-used in 14:19, 20, 22.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">The second and final Hebrew Bible mention of Melchizedek is in Psalm 110:4.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">The Lord hath sworn, and will not repent: 'Thou art a priest for ever after the manner of Melchizedek.'. (JPS 1917)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">11Q13 (11QMelch) is a fragment (that can be dated to the end of the 2nd or start of the 1st century BC) of a text about Melchizedek found in Cave 11 at Qumran in the Israeli Dead Sea area and which comprises part of the Dead Sea Scrolls.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">&nbsp;In this eschatological text, Melchizedek is seen as a divine being and Hebrew titles such as Elohim are applied to him. According to this text Melchizedek will proclaim the \"Day of Atonement\" and he will atone for the people who are predestined to him. He also will judge the peoples<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 26.4px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;
